Important News

Expected Date of Return to Europe by the League of Nations Investigation Team

▲ Compilation of Report Can be Completed as Expected

▲ Expected to Leave Beiping for Europe Around the Beginning of Next Month. Beiping Correspondence: The Investigation Team of the League of Nations is currently compiling its report and organizing the large number of documents it has collected for reference. The report is now being drafted, and the team deeply hopes that the report can be delivered to Geneva on September 15th as scheduled. However, some people in Europe believe that the resolution of the League of Nations General Assembly on July 1st to extend the six-month deadline for discussing the Sino-Japanese dispute (this deadline is set in accordance with Articles 12 and 15 of the League of Nations Covenant) is related to the progress of the Investigation Team's work. This is what those close to the Investigation Team are deeply surprised about. The feeling in Geneva seems to be that one of the reasons for the extension of the Article 12 deadline is due to the delay in the organization and departure of the Investigation Team, and the other is due to the slow progress of the Investigation Team's work. Some even believe that the Investigation Team requested an extension because it could not complete the report on schedule. However, according to the actual situation, this is not the case. The difficulty regarding the deadline issue is actually caused by the situation. When China initially appealed to the League of Nations, it invoked Article 11 of the Covenant. Only after the Investigation Team departed did China invoke the provisions of Article 15. Article 11 originally had no deadline or six-month limit. The restriction of Article 12 was caused by Article 15. It can be seen that the organization of the Investigation Team and its mission are based on Article 11. If the League of Nations had handled the investigation procedure in accordance with the provisions of Article 15, the group it selected would have been organized differently, its personnel would have been limited to those in the area, its powers would have been more limited, its report would have been narrower in scope, and the deadline would have been shorter. Now it is not the case. The scope of the Investigation Team's mission is very broad. Its task is not only to investigate the truth of a certain specific incident, but also to strive to promote Sino-Japanese relations. The Investigation Team should also study the background of the incident and examine the general situation in the Far East. This is necessary to understand the full picture of the incident.

In addition, the Investigation Team encountered major difficulties in the investigation process that it had to overcome. One of them was that the governments of the countries concerned, whether China or Japan, could not submit certain important documents to the Investigation Team before July or even early this month. Even though the Investigation Team's mission is extremely broad and the investigation work is extremely difficult, its report may still be compiled within the date originally scheduled for departure from Europe without being delayed. When the Investigation Team departed from Geneva, the League of Nations told all members that it did not expect the report to be completed before the end of August or the beginning of September. The budget for the Investigation Team's expenses stipulated in Geneva also stated that the Investigation Team's working period could be extended to nine months if necessary. It is also very reasonable for the League of Nations General Assembly to use the report drafted by the Investigation Team in accordance with Article 11 as a reference when it examines the Sino-Japanese incident in accordance with Article 15. Therefore, the League of Nations decided to extend its review period. How can it be said that it is due to the slow progress of the Investigation Team's work? The Investigation Team's work is proceeding as usual, and it is striving to complete it as soon as possible within the limits of the environment. It has not been delayed at all. In general, the Investigation Team will depart from Beiping in early September and return to Europe via Siberia. (Havas News Agency)

Journey to the West (Zhi Zhong)

▲ We Set Off Quickly

People who have long enjoyed the prosperity of the city resolutely braved the scorching heat and set off at 6:00 PM on August 11th, traveling tens of thousands of miles, crossing mountains and rivers, towards the northwest, which is generally regarded as a desolate and desolate place. No matter how terrible cholera is, they don't care. No matter how rampant bandits are, they don't care. Their only spirit and only aspiration is to conduct on-the-spot investigations in the northwest, develop the northwest, and protect the northwest, so that it will not become a continuation of the northeast. This is the only good news I think since the September 18th Incident. We don't want to lose the northeast. Our goal is to recover the northeast with all our might on the one hand and to defend the northwest with all our might on the other hand. The realization of the Shaanxi Industrial Investigation Team is the first step to complete this goal.

The Shaanxi Industrial Investigation Team was initiated and organized by the Longhai Railway Administration. All parties involved are experts with experience and specialized knowledge. As of the 10th, a total of 55 representatives from all parties have signed up to participate, which are disclosed separately as follows:

(A) Financial Sector: Li Guocai (Tianjin Deyuan Bank), Mao Yisheng (Tianjin Banking Association and Municipal Chamber of Commerce), Wang Yizun (Shanghai Banking Association), Bian Wenjian (Shanghai Banking Association), Fang Tongzi (Hankou Banking Association), Li Qing (China Agricultural and Industrial Bank)

(B) Industrial Sector: Xu Yihe (Suzhou, Zhejiang, Anhui Inland Flour Mill Association), Huang Xifan (Nantong Dasheng Yarn Factory)

(C) University Professors: Chen Zhi (Director of the Department of Forestry, Agricultural College, Northwest Association, Central University), Xu Nairen (Professor of Hydraulic Engineering, Department of Civil Engineering, College of Engineering, Central University), Li Tian (President of Tangshan College of Engineering, Jiaotong University), Li Guangzhong (Professor of Economics, Peiping Railway Management College, Jiaotong University), He Qingyun (Agricultural College, Central University), Li Deyi (Director of the Department of Forestry, Agricultural College, Jinling University), Sun Zhongyi (Lecturer, Agricultural College, Jinling University), Zhu Ruijie (Professor of the College of Engineering, Zhejiang University), Guo Weiping (Professor of the College of Education, Jinan University), Zhang Quan (Professor of the Department of Leather Science, Yanjing University), Yu Qianliu (Professor of the Department of Electrical Engineering, College of Engineering, Peiping University), Feng Jinglan (Professor of the Department of Mining, Beiyang Institute of Technology), Li Yongzhen (Director of the Department of Agriculture, Nantong College), Liu He (Professor of the Agricultural College, Peiping University), Zhao Renjun (Professor of the Department of Economics, Tsinghua University), Sun Tingzhong (Professor of the Jiaozuo Institute of Technology), Sun Yunzhu (Professor of the Department of Geology, Peking University), Chen Qingtang (Director of the Department of Dyeing and Weaving, Zhejiang University Senior Industrial Middle School)

(D) Press: Gu Zhizhong (Shanghai Newspaper Association), Wang Songnian (Tianjin Dagongbao), Zhang Liuyun (Hankou Wuhan Daily), Zhu Jingxin (Peiping Yishibao)

(E) Academic Groups: Zeng Jikuan (President of the Agricultural College, Peiping University, Chinese Agricultural Society), Zhou Ren (Chinese Science Society), Zhu Qiqing (Chinese Engineering Society), Huang Bokui (Chinese Mining Society), Hu Shuhua (Chinese Mining and Metallurgical Engineering Society), Shen Yiqian (China Industrial Federation)

(F) Local Chambers of Commerce: Hu Juewen (Shanghai Chamber of Commerce), Gao Bochang (Hankou Chamber of Commerce), Tianjin Chamber of Commerce is also represented by Mao Yisheng

(G) Government Officials: Xu Tinghu (Director of the Department of Agriculture, Ministry of Industry), Hu Boyuan (Technician, Ministry of Industry), An Han (Technician, Ministry of Industry), Yang Zhujun (International Trade Bureau, Ministry of Industry), Lu Chong (Technician, Ministry of Railways), Liu Binglun (Financial Department, Ministry of Railways), Li Xie (Committee Member of the Shaanxi Provincial Government), Wang Haibo (Legal Committee, Ministry of Communications), Wu Qi (Legal Committee, Ministry of Communications), Zhao Guobin (Geological Survey Institute, Shaanxi Construction Department), Ding Wenjiang (Geological Survey Institute, Ministry of Industry), Weng Wenhao (Geological Survey Institute, Ministry of Industry), Xiao Xingwu (Transportation Department, Longhai Railway Administration), Yu Zhonggang (Transportation Department, Longhai Railway Administration)

As of 4:00 PM on the 11th, the representatives from all walks of life counted on the southern group (those who went to the southern Shaanxi Road for investigation) included Xu Tinghu, An Han, Yang Zhujun, Lu Chong, Wang Haibo, Wu Qi, Zhao Guobin, Zhou Ren, Chen Zhi, Fang Tongzi, Hu Shuhua, Li Guangzhong, He Qingyun, Li Deyi, Guo Weiping, Zhang Quan, Liu He, Zhao Renjun, Sun Yunzhu, Sun Yanzhong, He Ziyuan, Wang Songnian, Huang Xifan, Xiao Xingwu, Yan Wei, Yang Min, etc., a total of thirty people. The northern route included Hu Boyuan, Liu Binglun, Ma Jin, Zhu Qiqing, Huang Bokui, Hu Juewen, Xu Nairen, Sun Zhongyi, Zhu Ruijie, Chen Qingtang, Gu Zhizhong, Yu Qianliu, Feng Jinglan, Li Yongzhen, Yu Zhonggang, Shen Yiqian, etc., about twenty-five people in total. The rest were unable to come due to illness or other reasons. I departed from Shanghai North Station at 9:25 AM on the 8th and traveled west. Originally, Mr. Wang Zhongwei had decided to go to Shaanxi a month ago to investigate the local social conditions. Unexpectedly, he had a fever the day before his departure and could not go west on the same train. The loneliness of the journey was greatly increased.

At 5:00 PM on the 8th, I arrived at the Jiangbian in Xiaguan, Nanjing. While taking the Chengping ferry across the Yangtze River, I unexpectedly met several comrades, including Hu Shuhua and Guo Weiping, who were "going to Shaanxi." When I arrived at Pukou, I took the ferry back to Xiaguan to change trains, repeating this back and forth, which resulted in me not being able to take the special express train that departed from Pukou at 7:00 PM that night. This made me feel very unhappy, but I was still able to cheer up and visit friends in the city and stayed there overnight.

The night passed quickly, and I got up early the next morning. After 8:00 AM, I took a car out of the city, crossed the river to Pukou, and took the special express train heading north at 10:00 AM to Xuzhou. After getting on the train, the weather was very hot, and all the passengers were sweating profusely, which was very uncomfortable. In addition, the train I was taking this time was the Jinpu train. Although it was nominally a special express train, it stopped at all stations, large and small, which greatly extended the time.

At about 9:30 PM, I arrived in Xuzhou. As soon as I got off the train, I was greeted by Stationmaster Xia. During the two hours in Xuzhou, I met Mr. Wang Yizun. He originally took the Pinghan Road to Zhengzhou, but the section of the line at Handan was washed away by the flood, and the train could not pass. He returned to Peiping and then from Peiping to Xuzhou.

We took the train west from Xuzhou at 12:30 AM. When we arrived in Kaifeng at about 11:00 AM the next morning, Mr. Hu Juewen got on the train from Kaifeng and met us. We talked and talked on the train. At 2:00 PM, we arrived at the meeting place in Zhengzhou. We were very grateful for all the hospitality we received in Zhengzhou. All the accommodation and food issues were resolved by the Longhai Railway Administration. On the evening of that day (the 10th), the colleagues of the road had a social gathering. On the morning of the 11th, the special party department of the road and the director Qian Zongze and Ling Hongxun gave a grand reception to all the members of the Shaanxi Industrial Investigation Team.

At 6:15 PM on the afternoon of the 11th, we, a group of more than 50 people, took a special train and set off westward again. According to the schedule, we could arrive at Tongguan at about 10:00 AM on the 12th. After arriving at Tongguan, we planned to take a car to Xi'an and arrive at our destination at about 7:00 PM in the evening.

On the morning of the 11th, it rained heavily, and the streets and alleys were almost flooded. Although the rain slowed down a little in the afternoon, it did not stop. The sky was gloomy, which reduced people's interest a lot, but our courage to work westward was absolutely not affected in the slightest. (To be continued)

Tianjin Zhongyuan Company Bombed

▲ A Bomb Was Found in the Makeup Department, but the Damage Was Minimal

▲ The Manager Said He Thought It Was Done by Patriotic Elements. Tianjin Correspondence: Since the September 18th Incident, the sales of Japanese goods in China have plummeted. However, in North China, the people's movement has been repeatedly suppressed, so that in the past three months, the Japanese goods market has returned to its original state, and profiteers only know how to make profits and do not know how to love the country. They often change the trademarks of Japanese goods to deceive their compatriots, which is especially hateful. Tianjin Zhongyuan Company is the largest department store. Customers are mostly affected by the plainclothes team directed by the Japanese, and the business is very depressed. Therefore, a branch was established on Huazhong Road in the French Concession. Recently, the business has improved slightly, while the main store in the Japanese Concession is still deserted. In the past two months, the fifth-floor theater and the rooftop garden have been restored, and tickets are only sold for two cents. Since July 15th, the main branch has held a one-month price reduction and offered a 3,000 yuan prize, and the business is booming. Unexpectedly, at 5:20 PM yesterday (the 14th), a bomb suddenly exploded in the cosmetics department on the ground floor of the main store, with a loud noise that was deafening. It happened to be Sunday, and there were many visitors. With the loud noise, the order was disrupted, and people fled in droves. The patrolling police officers urgently sounded the police whistle, and the Japanese police station was only a short distance away. Within three minutes of the bombing, the director of the station, Xinban, led the entire police force and ran forward. On the one hand, he cut off traffic on the roads around the company and searched everyone he met. On the other hand, he sealed the company's doors, wanting to conduct a detailed search. At this time, the tourists were still fleeing outward like a tide. Huang Wenqian, the manager of the company, was afraid that sealing the doors and searching would be embarrassing for the tourists, and the bomber had already disappeared. Even if he wanted to search, it would only cause trouble. So he repeatedly negotiated with Xinban and did not seal the doors and search. The disturbance lasted for an hour, and three suspects were arrested before traffic was restored. However, the news spread and shocked the city. In the evening, not only were there no customers in the theater and rooftop garden, but also the night market selling Japanese goods was deserted. The Japanese took the opportunity to make a fuss, thinking that this bomb had a political effect, and sent several Japanese soldiers to the roof of the company in the evening to look out over Chinese territory and sent armed military police to patrol back and forth in the Sino-Japanese border area. It can be said that it was just a waste of time. The cosmetics department of the company that was bombed has been completely repaired today (the 15th). The customers on the first, second, third, and fourth floors are as rare as morning stars. According to manager Huang Wenqian, yesterday afternoon at 5:00 PM, a customer bought a bottle of Xuehua Cream from Huang Jingxiang in the cosmetics department, which cost three cents and five cents. The customer gave a four-cent Mao ticket and asked the trainee Lin Chengye to take it to the main counter to get change. At this time, the buyer left a paper bag on the glass cabinet and left. Huang Jingxiang did not pay attention at first. When Lin Chengye returned from the main counter to get the change, he did not see the buyer, so he put the Xuehua Cream on the paper bag left behind and waited for him to pick it up. Unexpectedly, he used a little too much force, and the paper bag contained a bomb, which exploded immediately when hit. Lin Chengye was the closest to it, and half of his right side was injured by the explosion. Fortunately, the explosive force was not strong, so it did not affect others. Only a few pieces of glass in the cosmetics department were broken, and the damage was limited. Lin Chengye was immediately sent to the Common Hospital, where the shrapnel was taken out, and he will recover soon. As for the person who placed the bomb, some say he looked like a worker, and some say he was a young man in a suit. Because the shop assistants were very busy at the time, they did not pay close attention and could not judge. Huang also said that since the Tianjin Incident last year, the company was located in the Japanese Concession, so it had to set up a branch in the Concession to help itself. It was originally planned to close the main company, because it was afraid that more than 500 employees would lose their jobs and add a hidden worry to society. Recently, the business has improved slightly, and another incident occurred last night, which is really unfortunate. Outsiders suspect that the company is selling Japanese goods, which is a misunderstanding. If you investigate with the customs, you will understand. The unfortunate incident last night, I think it was done by patriotic elements, but I did not receive any prior warning. According to a gentleman in the business community, patriotic elements have recently organized a traitor-killing group and a Leifeng team, which often warn shops in writing. Hua Zhu Ni Rong Hao has been bombed once, and it is inevitable to be terrified. However, Japanese goods have not completely disappeared. A few days ago, the company published an advertisement in the newspaper to reply to the traitor-killing group, saying that it no longer sells Japanese goods. If you don't believe it, you can come and investigate. Whether Zhongyuan Company has received a warning, outsiders do not know. However, yesterday, it suddenly published a full-page advertisement in major newspapers, introducing domestic products. The intention can be imagined. The bombing of the shop is the third time for Zhongyuan. Therefore, the actions of the managers of the shops have been under strict martial law at all times. (August 15th)

Wang Lingji's Troops Repulse He Long's Remnant Bandits

▲ He Bandits' Night Attack on Shashi Thwarted

▲ Loss of Contact with Bandits in Honghu

Hankou Dispatch: He Long's remnant bandits, previously defeated by the 10th Army in conjunction with Sichuan troops, retreated to Honghu, but still plotted to harass western Hunan. Due to the National Army's blockade, they were unable to succeed. He Chengjun recently returned to Hankou after inspecting Yuekou, stating that he had ordered a large army to encircle Honghu and was determined to annihilate the bandits before the deadline set by Commander-in-Chief Chiang. Unexpectedly, He's bandits suddenly invaded Jingzhou and Shashi via a hidden route, making the situation very urgent. Fortunately, Wang Lingji, the Acting Commander-in-Chief of Bandit Suppression in the Upper Yangtze River area stationed in Shashi, quickly mobilized troops and repulsed them. On the 15th, Wang telegraphed a report to Hankou regarding the situation of repelling He's bandits, stating: "He's bandits, observing that our main forces were all at the front, daringly led the 3rd Regiment of the Pseudo 7th Division and the 2 Regiments of the Pseudo 8th Division themselves on the 13th, traveling secretly at night, departing from Longwan and Zhangjinhe, passing through Caojiachang and Jiangjiaqiao between Haoxue and Zifusi, and directly attacked Shashi. Upon receiving the report, I immediately ordered Regiment Commander Tong Yi and Regiment Commander Yang Huan to confront the enemy, and also ordered Regiment Yang stationed at Cenhekou and Zifusi, and Regiment Su stationed at Hougang and Shi Huibiao, to return to attack from the flanks. At dawn on the 14th, the bandits attacked in two routes, one at the Caoshi outside Jingzhou (i.e., Jiangling) city, which was bravely repelled by Battalion Chen of my Regiment Tong, and the other at Qinglongguan and Jinghua Temple east of Shashi, engaging in fierce battles with my Regiments Tong and Yang all day long. When my Regiment Yang stationed at Cenzi and Regiment Su stationed at Houshi attacked Jing-Sha from the bandit's flanks in the evening, the bandit's momentum was unsustainable, and they collapsed and retreated eastward along the original route in the middle of the night. In this battle, hundreds of bandits were killed and wounded, and their pseudo-division commander Wang Yiming was also wounded, and many were captured. In addition to sending teams to pursue, 'I also ordered the Luo Column to move south to intercept.'" It is now heard that the regiments led by He's bandits have lost contact with the bandits in Honghu. The National Army will separately encircle and annihilate them. The date of annihilation may not be far off. (August 16th)

Sixth Day of Continued Trial of the Noulens Case

▲ Noulens Roars in Court and is Ordered to Leave

▲ Prosecutor Reports on the Case's Progress

▲ Debate Concludes and Sentencing Set for the 19th

On the 17th, at 9:00 AM, the Jiangsu High Court continued to hear the case of the Noulens and Wang Delie endangering the Republic of China at the Nanjing Local Court. The judges present were the same as before. Lawyer Chen Ying was in the audience because Noulens had declared the revocation of his engagement yesterday, so he was not at the lawyer's seat when the court opened. After the judge took the stand, Noulens was brought to the court. Chief Judge Li Mian asked: "Yesterday, you stated that you did not want Lawyer Chen to defend you, so this court should appoint another lawyer. Do you want it or not?" Noulens replied: "According to Article 172 of the Criminal Procedure Law, I have already selected a lawyer to defend me on my behalf. The court cannot appoint one." (Asked) "Why did you not want him to defend you yesterday, and why do you want him to defend you today?" (Answered) "This is a right that the defendant should have. However, at this time, I don't want him to defend me. If necessary, I will still want him to defend me." (Asked) "This cannot be done casually. According to Article 56 of the Court Organization Law, the chief judge has the power to direct this. If you want him to defend you, he must perform his duties. If the previous power of attorney has been revoked, it must be re-entrusted. If it has not been revoked, it must be re-signed in the book for proof." So Noulens signed one after another. Lawyer Chen Ying then took the lawyer's seat, stating that on the one hand, he would abide by Chinese law and obey court rules without being used by the Communist Party, and on the other hand, he would perform his duties without violating the opinions of the defendant. At this point, Prosecutor Zhu Jun stood up to state the reasons for the prosecution in preparation for the start of the debate. Noulens disagreed, saying that the examination of the evidence had not been completed, and the defendant had not answered any opinions on the list of evidence, so the debate could not begin. (Asked) "If you have opinions and reasons, you will have the opportunity to state them at any time. The court does not refuse. Now that the evidence has been examined, the debate should of course begin." Noulens' attitude was strong and he kept clamoring, and order was almost disrupted. The judge said, "If you do not obey the order, you will suffer." Noulens' attitude became more stubborn. The court then ruled according to the obstruction of court order and ordered the bailiff to take him out of the court and押押回看守所中. He roared loudly as he left. Although Wang Delie was not as stubborn as Noulens, he also did not obey the court's order to maintain order, and was also ordered by the bailiff to be taken out and押回原所. The prosecutor then began to report, saying that before this case was solved, the Singapore authorities, after discovering the activities of the Communist Party in the East, notified the Shanghai Public Concession Bureau to conduct a secret investigation. After investigation, they found that post office box number 205 was commonly used by the Communist Party, and it was discovered that the user of this number, Er Sheng, was Noulens' alias, living at number 235 Sichuan Road, Shanghai. The Shanghai Police also discovered that Noulens often went to room 30, Block C, number 49 Nanjing Road. On June 15, 20th year [of the Republic], at 8:00 AM, Noulens was captured at number 235 Sichuan Road, and three bunches of keys were found on him, one bunch with thirteen keys, one bunch with eight keys, and one bunch with six keys, as well as one hundred and three yuan in banknotes. At that time, many envelopes and newspapers were also checked. Later, at room 30, Block C, number 49 Nanjing Road, many envelopes and newspapers were found, which were the same as those found at number 235 Sichuan Road. Later, one of the keys from the bunch of thirteen was used to open a small room. In addition to many stationery and clothing, three safes were found outside the room. The locksmith was hired to try these three bunches of keys one by one. As a result, two boxes were opened. In the second box, another key was found, which opened the third box. There were many Communist Party documents inside, totaling more than 600 pieces, of which 76 pieces were extremely related to endangering the Republic of China. This document can be divided into three categories: the first category is documents about the Chinese Communist Party's reports to the Communist Party leaders; the second category is documents of instructions and decrees from the Third International; the third category is documents that incite workers and peasants to direct the Red Army in Jiangxi, Hunan, Fujian, and other provinces to betray [the government]. (To be continued)

Sichuan Army's Tian Songyao Purchases Aircraft in Hong Kong

▲ Sixteen Aircraft in Total, Unable to be Transported to Sichuan

▲ Ma Qiyun's Detention in Guangdong

Guangzhou Dispatch: Tian Songyao, commander of the 29th Army of the Sichuan Army, recently sent Ma Qiyun to Hong Kong to order a batch of aircraft for the use of the army to organize an aviation team. Ma, whose family is from Taishan, Guangdong, studied aviation in the United States. After returning to China, he was ordered by Tian to purchase aircraft. After ordering sixteen combat aircraft with a flying speed of 210 meters per hour from the Hong Kong Lam Eun-jung Company, six were bombers, six were fighters, and four were trainers. However, after these aircraft were purchased, the Sichuan, Yunnan, and Guizhou authorities suddenly formed a new alliance, and Liu Xiang of Sichuan no longer seemed to be united with the southwest. The original plan was to transport Tian's aircraft to Sichuan via the Yangtze River through Chongqing, but Chongqing was Liu Xiang's territory, and Tian's aircraft might be detained if they passed through. Ma Qiyun then planned to open a new air route from Guangdong and Guangxi through Guizhou and directly to eastern Sichuan. If this route was open, the Tian army's aircraft in Hong Kong could all take off from Hong Kong without passing through Chongqing. Therefore, a Canadian pilot, 吉地氏, was hired in Hong Kong as an assistant. On the 8th, he flew a steel trainer aircraft and took off in Hong Kong. The itinerary was to take the route through Wuzhou and Liuzhou in Guangxi, cross Guiyang, and reach the eastern Sichuan Tian army defense area. The Guangxi Provincial authorities had been notified in advance to take care of the aircraft along the way. After Ma and others took off, they suddenly encountered headwinds, and resistance occurred during the flight. When they arrived at Wuzhou, they saw that the Wuzhou airfield was flooded, and they were forced to return to Guangzhou and landed at the Shougouling airfield. At that time, the Guangdong aviation personnel thought that Ma had come to Guangdong by plane without prior notice and suspected that there was something else going on. They flew to report to Chen Jitang. Chen was also suspicious and ordered the aircraft and the pilot to be detained. Then, an adjutant was sent from the headquarters to greet Ma Qiyun to the Commander-in-Chief's Office, where he was transferred to the Military Police Headquarters for detention. Ma's assistant, 吉地氏, thought that Ma was a formal commissioner of the Sichuan Army and was suddenly detained, so he visited Li Zongren to ask for rescue. Li knew that Ma was sent by Tian Songyao, so he interceded with Chen Jitang for Ma. At the same time, Bai Chongxi of Guangxi heard the news and also sent a telegram requesting bail. Chen Jitang then knew the inside story. The next day (9th) at 3:00 PM, he summoned Ma and explained the reason for the misunderstanding, saying that this incident was due to a telegram from Liu Xiang in advance, and showed Liu's telegram, which stated that Ma was a communist. After Ma was released, he flew the original aircraft back to Hong Kong on the 11th. According to Ma, although he encountered setbacks this time, he was still determined to test the new air route between Guangxi, Guizhou, and Sichuan. After ten or eight days, he would plan to fly back to Sichuan again in order to safely transport the purchased aircraft back to eastern Sichuan. (August 12th)

Shantou Business Community Opposes Business Tax

▲ Organizing a Committee Against Business Tax

▲ Resolving to Prepare for a General Strike

Shantou Dispatch: Since the Financial Department appointed Hu Guannan as the Director of the Shantou Business Tax Bureau, the business community has risen up in opposition, and a meeting was held at the Chamber of Commerce to decide to telegraph the province to request a postponement of the tax, citing the people's hardship. However, after this telegram was sent, more than ten days passed without any response. Hu Guannan further decided to open the business as ordered, and those who failed to comply within the time limit would be punished in accordance with the regulations. The merchants were panic-stricken. Yesterday (7th) at 2:00 PM, another meeting was held at the Chamber of Commerce. Many representatives attended the meeting, and reporters were politely refused to attend, so it was not easy to know the content of the resolutions. However, it was heard that the strike movement had been decided, and the Remittance Association, the Silver Industry Association, the Medicinal Materials Association, the Jiangsu-Guangdong Association, the Silk Cloth Association, the North-South Port Goods Transportation Association, the Match Association, the Brokerage Association, the Tourism Association, the Liquor Association, the Restaurant Association, the 洋糖 Association, the Miscellaneous Grain Association, and other thirteen groups were designated as the Committee Against Business Tax. It was also voted to temporarily suspend the payment of business tax until the government abolished various harsh taxes and miscellaneous levies. The city's fifty-one businesses, together with those who did not fill out the report and obtain a license, if the Business Tax Bureau imposed a fine, they would paste the "Permanently Closed" sign on the door and automatically strike. It was heard that the Business Tax Bureau saw that the attitude of the merchants was激昻, and few people went to fill out the report and obtain a license. On the 8th, the Business Tax Bureau changed its attitude and announced an extension of ten days, from the 9th to the 18th. If the merchants still did not fill out the report and obtain a license, they would be punished. Judging from the situation, the business community did not seem willing to submit. (August 9th)

Judge Zhou opened the court for a mass trial several times, and the case was already clear, but the witness surnamed Xu had not been arrested, which delayed the conclusion for several months. The debate was finally concluded a few days ago, and the verdict was scheduled to be announced yesterday. Huang Ma and Zhang Guisheng were sentenced to death for jointly plotting murder. Huang Rongdao was sentenced to 15 years of imprisonment for jointly plotting murder. Wang Qishun and Sun Guangfa were found not guilty.

Shen Bao Education News

Special Issue on the National Sports Conference

The National Sports Conference Held its Second Morning Plenary Session, Resolving Six Sports Objectives; Afternoon Review; Evening Banquet by He Yingqin; Yesterday Was the Second Day of the National Sports Conference. The Second General Assembly Was Held at 8:00 AM. Chairman Zhang Zhijiang. Each Group Reported on the Results of Their Review. The Reports Concluded at Approximately 12:00 PM. The Assembly Decided On: (1) Sports Objectives (2) Each Group to Submit a General Report for Discussion by the Assembly (3) Establishment of a Committee for Compiling a Draft Plan for National Physical Education Implementation. In Addition to the Original Drafters Serving as Ex-Officio Members, Six Other Members Were Elected. In the Afternoon at 2:00 PM, Each Group Held a Separate Review Meeting, and Each Group Nominated Shang Shude, Zhang Huilan, Wu Bangwei, Dong Shouyi, Wang Zipei, and Wu Tunan as Representatives to the National Physical Education Implementation Plan Compilation Committee. At 7:00 PM, He Yingqin Hosted a Banquet for All Members at the Lixingshe. Today, Review Meetings Will Be Held in the Morning and Afternoon, and the Third General Assembly Will Be Held Tomorrow Morning. The Details of Yesterday Are Recorded Below.

Second General Assembly

Adoption of Six Sports Objectives; Organization of a Compilation Committee

▲Opening Ceremony

Nanjing, 17th Telegram - The National Sports Conference was held on the 17th starting at 8 o'clock, and the situation is as follows:

Of the 102 members actually present, specially appointed member Niu Yongjian also arrived (Wang Zhengyan and Wu Siyu were still absent, and the Minister and Vice Minister of Education were not present). Gu Shusen, a member of the preparatory committee, returned to Nanjing from Jiangxi and attended for the first time. Deputy Speaker Zhang Zhijiang chaired the meeting. Secretary Wu Yan and Zhong Lingxiu of the conference sat to the left and right of the chairman, assisting with the record of proceedings. Gong Weitao, Huang Longxian, Sun Shaobo, and Zhang Boyin. After the meeting began as scheduled, the chairman reported:

▲Chairman Zhang Zhijiang's Report

China's Greatest Malady Lies in Weakness

Three Points to Note During Discussions on Proposals

Zhang said in his report: Speakers say that China's greatest problems are weakness and poverty. Weakness leads to poverty; the former is the cause, the latter is the effect. Weakness is the cause, poverty is the result. China's economic status is unequal, dependent on others, controlled by others, and at the mercy of others. The reason for our own numbness, paralysis, hemiplegia, being bedridden and on our last breath, the biggest reason is weakness. The great malady is weakness, and the key is weakness. If we do not catch up and treat this great illness, and only use other methods to seek economic development and equality of economic status, it will be like climbing a tree to catch fish or waiting for a rabbit to run into a tree. The more we seek, the further away we get. Therefore, the fundamental solution is to strive for strength, restore health, and promote national sports for everyone. If we can do this, equality of status can be expected soon. Therefore, we very much hope that financial experts and medical experts will participate in our conference. I have summarized the opinions expressed by the representatives at yesterday's opening ceremony into three points for your reference when discussing proposals:

(1) Suitable for Chinese national character (2) Use the most economical and convenient methods to promote (3) Strive for universalization of sports, that is, popularization. Please pay attention to the above three points.

Reports on Review Results from Each Group

(1) Sports Objectives Group

Document Clerk Shang Shumei Reports

—Discussion Opinions—

1. Du Tingxi argued that there were too many proposals and too little time, so the entire goal should be discussed and not each item individually.

2. Chu Minyi argued that there were many proposals and that the opinions of the review committee should be respected. The review committee should put forward its overall opinions for discussion by the assembly. If there are no objections, it should be passed immediately. If there are objections, it should be sent back for review.

3. Xu Zhiyi argued that after discussing the objectives set in the plan and the review results of the proposals, it should be handed over to the preparatory committee for compilation.

4. Wang Yaoan argued that the objectives set in the plan should be supplemented with proposals to create a complete goal, which should be compiled by the plan drafting committee.

5. Chen Jianai and Sun Mingxiu argued that the meeting procedures should be followed.

6. Chu Minyi argued that the review results of each group should be reported to the assembly, handed over to the three plan drafters, and then four people should be elected by the assembly (or the chairmen of each group should serve) to re-compile the plan and submit it to the assembly for approval.

7. Lin Yinnan agreed with Chu.

8. Jin Zhaojun argued that the review committee should elect people to compile it. After passing, elect other people to compile it. After multiple people, it was seconded and put to a vote. (Resolution passed).

The chairman put Chu's proposal principle, that is, each group should report the review results to the assembly, followed by discussion, and then elect the compilation committee.

1. Hao Gengsheng argued that six people should be elected by the assembly to handle it together with the three plan drafters.

2. Chen Panling argued that people should be elected from each review group, plus the drafting committee members.

3. Chu Minyi seconded Chen Panling's method, but the administrative group with the most people should nominate two people, and the remaining four groups should nominate one person each, along with the three plan drafting committee members, for a total of nine people.

4. Xu Yan agreed with Chu.

5. Su Jing, Chen Boqing, Zhang Xinfu, Chen Jianai, and Du Tingxi spoke successively to supplement.

(2) To train the nation's ability to use their bodies to adapt to the environment

(3) To cultivate the spirit of national cooperation and solidarity

(4) To promote national spirit and cultivate a national atmosphere of chivalry and bravery

(5) To cultivate national habits of sports, games, and entertainment

Martial Arts Film Screening

The performers wore headscarves and armor, shouted to cheer each other on during the competition, and their voices were as fierce as tigers. The winner was determined by striking the head, thrusting the throat, slashing the waist, and splitting the wrist, winning two out of three times. There were many wonderful moments during the performance, which won a lot of applause.

Expert Talk

Ma Liang Talks About Chinese New Martial Arts

The sports of each country have their own characteristics, and their methods are also different. China has never had a fixed method. Based on my decades of experience, I have created Chinese New Martial Arts, which is a Chinese-style sports movement. Chinese New Martial Arts is divided into four items: unarmed, divided into boxing and wrestling; weapons, divided into sticks and swords. Elementary school students must learn boxing. Middle school students and people over 40 or 50 years old learn wrestling. Wrestling is enough to strengthen the body. Theory and experience are equally important. Whether you can do it or not is shown in the fight. As for sticks, I argue that everyone, regardless of gender or age, must have a stick for self-defense. Swordsmanship is most suitable for the intellectual class. Swordsmen have the style of a gentleman.

Draft National Physical Education Implementation Plan (3)

B. Secondary Schools

(1) Grounds—

In addition to removing the areas marked with an "X" in the primary school grounds, the following grounds should be added:

Tennis Courts: Four, approximately 34,000 square feet in total.

Soccer Field: One, approximately 50,000 square feet.

Track and Field Ground: One, approximately 80,000 square feet. The soccer field can be included within the track and field ground, but the running track should not be less than 300 meters; otherwise, it cannot include a soccer field. The above-mentioned grounds are the minimum requirements for secondary schools with fewer than 100 students. For secondary schools with more than 100 students, the area should be doubled for every 100 students, and half of the area can be added at the discretion for those with less than 50 students (but the soccer field and track and field ground should be doubled for every 300 students).

If the school site is close to a public sports ground, the track and field ground in the public sports ground can be fully utilized to reduce the addition of track and field grounds in the school. However, the establishment of a track and field ground in the school should not be completely omitted because of public facilities.

(2) Fixed Equipment—

In addition to removing the items marked with an "X" in the primary school fixed equipment, the following fixed equipment should be added:

Vaulting Box: One X

Jump Over Apparatus (Small Wooden Horse): Two

Wooden Horse: Two

Mats (made of canvas and cotton): Four X

Balance Beam: One X

Pick-Up Race Box: Four

Vaulting Platform: One

Parallel Bars: One

Horizontal Bar (height can be adjusted at will): Two X

Rope Circle: One set

Fixed Equipment for Track and Field:

Shot Put Circle: Two

Shot Puts: Two

Discus Throwing Circle: One

Hurdles: Sixty

Pole Vaulting Stands: One pair

Landing Pit (including pole vaulting, high jump, and long jump): Three

Soccer Goals: One pair

Starting Gun: One

The above-mentioned fixed equipment is the minimum requirement for secondary schools with fewer than 100 students. For secondary schools with more than 100 students, the number should be doubled for every 100 students, and half of the number can be added at the discretion for those with less than 50 students. However, the soccer goals, hurdles, and pole vaulting stands should be doubled for every 300 students.

(3) Consumable Equipment—

In addition to the consumable equipment for primary schools listed above, the following consumable equipment should be added:

Soccer Balls: Four

Discus: Two

Javelins: Twelve

Pole Vaulting Poles: Four

Crossbars: Twenty

Stopwatches: Four

Starting Guns and Ammunition: One hundred and fifty

Tennis Balls: Two dozen

The above-mentioned consumable equipment is the minimum standard per semester for secondary schools with fewer than 100 students. For secondary schools with more than 100 students, the number should be doubled for every 100 students, and half of the number can be added at the discretion for those with less than 50 students. However, the stopwatches, starting guns, and ammunition should be doubled for every 300 students.

C. Universities and Colleges

(Grounds)—

Same as secondary schools, but the number of tennis courts should be increased appropriately within the possible range.

(2) Fixed Equipment—

Same as secondary schools, but the items marked with an "X" in the secondary school fixed equipment can be reduced appropriately.

(3) Consumable Equipment—

Same as secondary schools.

D. Public Sports Grounds

(1) Grounds—

The number of grounds should be the sum of those required for universities, colleges, primary schools, and secondary schools, and a portion should be designated for women's sports. This is the minimum requirement. If the local population is large and there are many participants in sports, the grounds should be increased appropriately according to the local financial resources. In particular, children's playgrounds should be established in separate areas outside the main grounds. The problem with public sports grounds in the country today is not the insufficient number of grounds but the lack of concrete facilities.

(2) Fixed Equipment—

The number of fixed equipment should be the sum of that required for universities, colleges, primary schools, and secondary schools. Swimming pools are currently lacking in the country and should be gradually established.

(3) Consumable Equipment—

The number of consumable equipment should be the sum of that required for universities, colleges, primary schools, and secondary schools.

The above-mentioned equipment are all outdoor facilities. Physical activities should be held outdoors as much as possible. However, China has a vast territory, and the climate, wind, sand, and rainfall vary from place to place. Indoor physical education facilities are also necessary for most areas. Regardless of whether it is a university, college, primary school, secondary school, or public sports ground, the area of the indoor sports ground must be at least large enough to accommodate one basketball court or one volleyball court. The size should be determined based on the economic situation. As for the construction method, in addition to the amount of funding, it must also be determined based on the climate. The education departments of each province should conduct research on their respective regions and make detailed regulations.

(3) Funding

There is no doubt that national physical education should be vigorously promoted in China after years of weakness. However, in recent years, the promotion of physical education by the Chinese people has lacked an overall plan, resulting in two phenomena. First, the central government and wealthy cities spend huge sums of money to build large-scale sports grounds and organize various athletes' sports meets to showcase their achievements in promoting sports. Second, inland areas are affected by natural disasters and man-made disasters, and funding is insufficient. The state of sports facilities is rudimentary, almost non-existent. Both of these extremes are not the true way to promote sports. Wealthy areas should not be surprised by false names, and impoverished areas should know the need for physical education. Each should consider the local situation and take promoting universal sports suitable for the national conditions as the standard, and prepare a corresponding budget to avoid the drawbacks of one side squandering public funds and the other side making empty promises. Considering the conditions in various places, the minimum amounts for the funding of schools and public sports grounds at all levels are roughly as follows. The central and local administrative budgets must be prepared properly by the competent authorities according to the circumstances. I will not elaborate on this here.

The funding for purchasing and repairing grounds and fixed equipment for schools and public sports grounds at all levels should be based on the value of the various equipment purchased locally. Although the purchase value of various fixed and consumable equipment is not exactly the same in various places, the actual difference is very small. The following principles are established and can be reduced proportionally. Those with fewer than fifty people will still be counted as fifty people.

Public sports grounds: 400 yuan per year for practitioners. If this number is exceeded, it should be increased proportionally.

(4) Methods of Promoting Physical Education

(1) Research Work: The materials, methods, and standards adopted for the implementation of physical education should be reliable and appropriate only after research procedures. Therefore, research is the first step in promoting physical education. Neglecting it is like a blind man riding a blind horse, and I am afraid that he will go astray. The research institutions can have the following types:

(1) Designate the physical education department of a national university as a research institution. Its funding can be subsidized by the Cultural Foundation or the Ministry of Education to add research professors.

(2) The Cultural Foundation establishes a physical education lectureship to assist the physical education department of a certain university in research work.

(3) Designate domestic educational research and experimental institutions to add a physical education research department, and its funding shall be subsidized by the Ministry of Education.

(4) Select model cities and towns and villages as physical education experimental zones.

(5) National Martial Arts Museum

B. Research Matters

(1) Physical Education Curriculum for Male and Female Schools at All Levels: The former Ministry of Education had set physical education curriculum standards for senior and junior high schools and primary schools, but there were no detailed particulars. After compiling and designating schools to implement experiments and obtaining satisfactory results, it will be announced and adopted. In the future, experts should be invited to revise the details and engage in trials.

(2) Physical Education Examination Standards: To seek the popularity of physical education, there must be an examination method to examine the performance of students in schools and public sports in the country. However, due to the large number of schools and people, the method must be simple. For each person's performance in each item, only reaching a certain standard is required. This standard must come from measurement and statistics, and it cannot be arbitrarily determined. This standard takes a long time to succeed.

Members visit the Central Sports Ground (photographed in Nanjing Guanghua)

###

(3) National Martial Arts: The value, the similarities and differences of schools, the methods of teaching and competition, and the position in physical education must be jointly studied by national martial artists and sports educators to form an overall plan.

(4) Rural Sports: 85% of the national population lives in the countryside and are mostly farmers. Whether they have spare time to engage in physical education and what kind of activities suit their tastes should be investigated and researched on the spot.

(5) Urban Public Sports: Collect existing folk sports activities, improve them, and promote them. Adopt foreign public sports activities, adapt them to the Chinese environment, and utilize them flexibly.

(Other)

(2) Training of Talents: The ideal institution for training talents is the physical education research institution, such as the Institute of Biology in the capital. Many biologists in China are trained by the institute. However, research institutions cannot be established in large numbers, and all talents cannot be trained by research institutions. Therefore, separate standards for curriculum and training institutions must be established.

A. Curriculum for Physical Education Teacher Training: Chinese society is affected by politics, and the economy is increasingly depleted. University students study at school for many years, and their families bear a heavy burden. It is difficult for the physical education departments of universities in China to recruit enough students, and many drop out due to economic constraints. Therefore, the physical education curriculum must be flexible, dividing the four-year curriculum into two sections. In the first two years, attention is paid to compulsory courses, and in the last two years, attention is paid to elective courses so that students from poor families can leave school halfway to take up teaching positions and then return to school to continue their studies. Then, their experience is rich, their learning ability is increased, and the knowledge they acquire is more practical. The distribution of the curriculum is as follows:

Xia Yuanqi Does Not Want to Represent Pingda

Beiping, 17th. Xia Yuanqi does not want to serve as acting principal of Pingda and will resign at the end of the month.

Record of the 17th Annual Meeting of the China Science Society

▲ To restore the inherent culture of the Northwest

▲ Held in Chang'an, a remote place in the western frontier

The current annual meeting of the China Science Society was held in Chang'an, Shaanxi. It was prepared in advance by Chang'an members Li Yizhi, Shou Tianzhang, and Li Yan. Members from Beijing, Shanghai, Pingjin and other places arrived in Chang'an one after another, including Wang Qi, Chen Yanshan, Shen Lianghua, Lu Minxing, Ge Suicheng, Zhou Zijing, Xu Nanfei, Sun Yanzhong, Yu Qianliu, Sun Yun, Zhu Qiqing, Li Yongzhen, Hu Shuhua, Hu Boyuan, Feng Jinglan, and Chang'an members Li Yizhi, Shou Tianzhang, Li Yan, Yang Heqing, and more than 20 other people. The opening ceremony was held at the Xunzhen Building of the Civil Affairs Department on the afternoon of August 13. First, Li Yizhi, the president of the annual meeting, delivered the opening speech, which roughly stated that the society had been established for 20 years. The previous 16 annual meetings were mostly held in coastal ports. Now, in order to popularize scientific knowledge, the society held the meeting in Chang'an, a remote place in the Northwest, and also sought to restore and expand the inherent culture of the Northwest. He also hoped that in the future, the military conference would gradually be held in the inland. Then Yang Hucheng, the honorary president of the annual meeting, delivered a speech on behalf of the chairman, briefly stating that Chang'an was located in a remote place in the western frontier and had few opportunities to come into contact with science. The comrades of the China Science Society were very admired for coming to Shaanxi from afar, regardless of the heat and fear of the tiger epidemic. Then the president, Wang Qi, reported on the general situation of the society, briefly stating that the society's purpose was to investigate things and extend knowledge, utilize resources to benefit the people, engage in research on the one hand, and apply the results of the research to society on the other. Due to limited financial resources, the society's work over the years has not been fully developed, but the Mingfu Library and the Institute of Biology in Beijing have been built, and 16 volumes of scientific journals and various scientific series have been published, which also made considerable contributions. There are more than 1,000 members, divided into four groups: materials, biology, engineering, and society. Although the number of people is limited, they are working hard and have great hopes. He also hoped that all walks of life would support them so that scientific knowledge could be popularized among the people, and then Chinese science would have achievements. For example, at yesterday's (i.e., the day before yesterday's) meeting of the Executive Yuan, the ministers elected Minister He as the chairman. This time, Vice President Song returned to Beijing. Before the candidate for the President of the Executive Yuan is determined, he must concurrently serve as the President of the Executive Yuan according to law. As for the change of the President of the Executive Yuan this time, the ministers will not change, because according to the responsible cabinet system, if the policy cannot be implemented, the entire cabinet will resign, but it will never advance or retreat together because of the departure or stay of the President of the Executive Yuan. Customs Inspection of Domestic Port Goods: Shipping Companies Strongly Oppose

After the domestic port ships in Shanghai loaded import and export goods, the cent tax was abolished last year, and no tax was levied, and the goods were also exempted from inspection. Recently, the Jianghai Customs suddenly announced that all domestic port goods must be inspected and imposed huge fines on the Datada's unified tax on native cloth that was leaked from inspection, which aroused the opposition of all shipping companies in Shanghai. The situation is quite激昂. The situation is recorded as follows:

▲ Tax Exemption Measures

It is customary for ships traveling to domestic ports to be managed by the Jianghai Customs together with civilian ships. The imported goods reported and loaded have always been subject to simple inspection procedures by the South City Shipping Association at the Datada Wharf, and the goods are reported by the shipping company on its behalf, and the summary sheet is submitted to the Customs for inspection. This has been followed for a long time. On June 1 last year, the Ministry of Finance ordered that all 50-mile regular customs be cancelled, renamed branches, and all taxes were exempted. Import and export goods only need to be reported and do not need to be inspected. Shipping has been very convenient for a year.

▲ New Customs Inspection Rules

On June 23 this year, the General Tax Department instructed that all domestic port ships entering and leaving the port must be inspected. Export goods must not be loaded on ships before inspection, and import goods must not be unloaded ashore in advance before inspection. Imports on Sundays and closing days are allowed to be unloaded in advance except for livestock and fresh goods. All other goods are allowed to be unloaded in the Qianfang and wait for inspection the next day. All must abide by this.

▲ Datada Fine

After the fact was implemented, on July 30, the first iron barge of Datada Company, Hengda, transported various goods from Tongzhou. Among them, there were 200 pieces of native cloth with a unified tax bill. At 11:00 a.m., someone came to Hengda to inspect. The workers and boatmen mistakenly thought it was a customs officer inspecting. And the cloth customers wanted to take it away urgently because the goods were crowded and the tide was falling. The workers thought that the inspection had been completed and allowed them to be picked up. At 3:30 p.m., the customs inspector came to find out that the person who came to inspect first was a member of the Unified Tax Bureau, and there was no way to bring back what had been taken away. The Customs considered it a violation of the regulations and fined 200 taels of silver. Datada stated the misunderstanding and requested exemption from the fine, but it was not approved.

▲ Shipping Companies Oppose

This time, all the shipping companies in Shanghai's domestic port shipping companies, such as Zhenda, Datada, Datong, Jufeng, etc., convened a meeting and unanimously stated that the import and export of domestic port ships are all opened on the same day, and the minimum time to stay is short. When imported goods arrive at the wharf, they must be rushed to pick up, and livestock and fresh goods are especially easy to die and rot. It is extremely difficult to inspect import goods. If unloading is not allowed before inspection, it is actually very difficult to handle. Moreover, the goods are piled up in one place in the ship's cabin, which is messy and cluttered. Inspection takes time, and there is only one customs officer. If you want to inspect a large number of ships, you will not come to inspect until 3:00 or 4:00 p.m. It is inevitable that the ship will not be able to clear customs on the same day because of the inspection, and who will be responsible for the loss of the ship's schedule? If the import goods can be inspected before 3:00 or 4:00 p.m., the export goods will not be able to catch up with the loading. If passengers and goods are stranded and want to be loaded, and the ship cannot be opened, isn't it because of this that they will fall into a dilemma? Moreover, the inspection is only based on personal intentions, without any clear written regulations, and there is no preparation at all, which is especially painful.

▲ Request to Cancel

The Shanghai Aviation Association stated in detail that the inspection of import and export goods in inland rivers is extremely difficult to handle in fact, and that Datada barges holding unified tax bills have never been inspected, which has become a custom. This matter was also due to a misunderstanding. With regard to goods that do not need to be taxed, the Customs now makes a rash decision based on a notice, regardless of whether there are any obstacles or whether the shipping companies can comply with it, and forcibly fines huge sums of money for goods that do not need to be taxed. Is this not a case of harsh government being fiercer than a tiger? Merchants will not be in danger. The Customs has not yet gained any benefits, but the shipping companies have already suffered losses. Is this what the government should do when it is advocating to restore shipping rights and promote shipping? This matter is a pain in the flesh for domestic port shipping companies. For this reason, we request the Aviation Association to quickly forward it to the Jianghai Customs to immediately cancel the inspection of imports and exports in domestic ports to facilitate shipping. (Omitted below) It is also heard that if the shipping companies do not achieve their goals, they will make a final and determined statement.

Retailers Should Clearly Mark the Origin of Goods

▲The Best Way to Boycott Japanese Goods

▲A Westerner's Letter Published in the "Continental Daily News"

Yesterday, a Westerner, Mr. Walrer C. Youngs, sent a letter to the "Continental Daily News" stating that after Japan loses its huge market in China, its military adventures in China will become financially impossible due to the import surplus. However, radical and forced boycotts of Japanese goods can easily provoke incidents. If the public's patriotic sentiment is used to vigorously oppose aggressive countries, they will eventually succumb. In short, the power to control life and death rests with the end-users, not with wholesalers and importers. Unfortunately, today's consumers often do not know the origin of goods when purchasing them. However, the remedy is very simple and cannot be opposed by Japan or other countries. All public associations, business firms, and groups across the country only need to agree that all retail goods must be marked with their place of origin, such as "Made in USA", "Made in England", or "Made in Japan". At that time, the power will be transferred to the Chinese people. If the people do not buy Japanese goods for any reason, they can prevent retailers from continuing to purchase Japanese goods from wholesalers. Then, other foreign merchants can take the opportunity to fill the gap created by this legitimate boycott, and Japan will have to abandon its illusions. The international banditry behavior they are engaging in is no longer appropriate for the present time and was abandoned in the 19th century.

Japanese Commercial Revival Association Speculates on Merchants' Psychology

▲Proposes Two Ways to Deal with the "Blood Soul Anti-Treason Squad"

According to the Shih Wen News Agency, since the Shanghai War settlement was officially signed, various Japanese commercial organizations in Shanghai have organized a Commercial Revival Committee to plan for commercial recovery. They also appointed representatives Yuukichi Hayashi, Masataka Mimura, Zenji Izumi, Rokuzaburo Shiraishi, and others to return to Japan to petition their government, requesting compensation of 7.5 million yuan for the losses caused by the invasion of Shanghai. However, they have not yet received a satisfactory response from the government, so Yuukichi Hayashi and others are still staying in Tokyo, awaiting the government's final reply. At 5:00 PM the day before yesterday, the committee convened a meeting at the conference room of the Japanese Residents' Association to seek a quick solution to this issue. Because Chairman Yuukichi Hayashi had not returned from Japan, Consul-General Murai, stationed in Shanghai, was publicly elected as chairman. The meeting ended at 9:00 PM. It is reported that, in addition to sending another telegram to the representatives petitioning in Japan, Yuukichi Hayashi and others, urging them to actively liaise with all sectors in the country and request the government to quickly compensate the Chinese merchants for losses in Shanghai, they also decided to draft a declaration and a policy for the revival of trade with China. As for how to deal with the activities of the "Blood Soul Anti-Treason Squad", the committee also proposed two methods, positive and negative. Because Consul-General Murai will leave office and return to his country at the end of this month, all the above documents are prepared to be taken back to his country by Murai and presented to the government for review. The Shih Wen News Agency reporter, in order to clarify the content of the two measures, negative and positive, proposed by the Japanese Commercial Revival Committee at the meeting to deal with the activities of the "Blood Soul Anti-Treason Squad", tried to find out the content as follows:

▲Negative Aspect: Chinese merchants have always held the principle of high profits. This can be confirmed in previous movements to boycott Japanese goods. Now, Chinese merchants are withdrawing goods one after another due to the activities of the "Blood Soul Anti-Treason Squad". We merchants should urgently seek all practical methods to remedy this situation, and we should not be afraid to sacrifice capital and allow goods to pile up. The tentatively drafted negative remedies are as follows: (1) Increase the commission to make Chinese brokers loyal to their duties and able to find ways to sell the goods they are responsible for. Therefore, we should immediately decide to increase their commission to 40% (for example, if the price of the goods is 100 yuan, then the commission is 40 yuan). In this way, we can ensure that Chinese brokers will not avoid difficulties or dangers and will do their best to sell the goods. (2) Reduce costs. Most Chinese merchants are greedy for high profits. If we can reduce the cost of various goods as much as possible and trade with them, they will be happy to do so. Even if the "Blood Soul Anti-Treason Squad" is active, it will not shake the foundation of their trade with us. For example, if the cost of a certain item, including shipping, tariffs, and other miscellaneous expenses, actually exceeds three francs, we may as well reduce the selling price to two and a half francs. Although the capital has been sacrificed, this is the only way to make Chinese merchants happy to sell. (3) Be responsible for delivery. The activity of the "Blood Soul Anti-Treason Squad" has made Chinese merchants who sell our goods feel disheartened. If the goods are intercepted by these people on the way, not only will the capital be completely sacrificed, but they will also be accused of being traitors. Therefore, if we want to restore the sale of goods, we should set up a delivery department to be responsible for delivering the goods to the Chinese merchant's receiving point. As for the method of sales, we should also provide guidance to strengthen their determination to sell.

▲Positive Aspect: Protecting the foreign trade of overseas Chinese merchants is the responsibility of the local military and political authorities. The government should also provide practical assistance. The "Blood Soul Anti-Treason Squad" has been active everywhere for more than a month. In this month or so, the losses suffered by our overseas Chinese merchants in various places have been shocking, and we have not yet heard that the government and the military and political authorities in Shanghai have lodged a practical protest with the Chinese municipal government to stop and ban them, sitting idly by as the business of overseas Chinese merchants declines day by day. Now, in order to remedy the situation, (1) the government authorities should directly lodge a serious protest with the Chinese government, and at the same time, strictly order the consuls stationed in various places to immediately negotiate with the highest local Chinese authorities if they find the "Blood Soul Anti-Treason Squad" and to take effective measures to protect the foreign trade of the local overseas Chinese merchants. (2) The severe decline in foreign trade is enough to shake the foundation of the domestic economy. Therefore, if the negotiation is ineffective and the "Blood Soul Anti-Treason Squad" is still rampant everywhere, further measures should be taken to protect the interests of overseas Chinese merchants and at the same time consolidate the foundation of the domestic economy. As for what the effective methods are, the government should solemnly decide.
